159	
160	def perform_import(val, setting_name):
161	    """
162	    If the given setting is a string import notation,
163	    then perform the necessary import or imports.
164	    """
165	    if val is None:
166	        return None
167	    elif isinstance(val, str):
168	        return import_from_string(val, setting_name)
169	    elif isinstance(val, (list, tuple)):
170	        return [import_from_string(item, setting_name) for item in val]
171	    return val
172	
173	
174	def import_from_string(val, setting_name):
175	    """
176	    Attempt to import a class from a string representation.
177	    """
178	    try:
179	        return import_string(val)
180	    except ImportError as e:
181	        msg = "Could not import '%s' for API setting '%s'. %s: %s." % (val, setting_name, e.__class__.__name__, e)
